group storage versions mapping v1beta1 to v1 through a multi-layered infrastructure:\\n\\n## Core Infrastructure Components\\n\\n**1. ResourceEncodingConfig (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go)**\\nThe ResourceEncodingConfig interface defines how API resources are stored in etcd. The DefaultResourceEncodingConfig implementation maintains a mapping of GroupResources to their storage versions via SetResourceEncoding(). The StorageEncodingFor() method returns which GroupVersion should be used for etcd storage, while the BackwardCompatibileStorageEncodingFor() method provides compatibility-aware version selection based on the effective Kubernetes version.\\n\\n**2. StorageVersion Manager (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storageversion/manager.go)**\\nThe Manager interface tracks which storage versions are in use and manages their updates. The ResourceInfo struct contains encoding information including DirectlyDecodableVersions and ServedVersions, allowing the system to track multiple versions even when only one is used for storage.\\n\\n**3. Storage Factory (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/storage_factory.go)**\\nDefaultStorageFactory uses ResourceEncodingConfig to determine the storage version for resources. The NewConfig() method calls StorageEncodingFor() or BackwardCompatibileStorageEncodingFor() to determine which GroupVersion to use when persisting objects to etcd.\\n\\n**4. StorageVersionProvider Interface (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/rest.go)**\\nAn optional interface allowing storage implementations to disclose their storage version via StorageVersion() method.\\n\\n## REST Storage Provider Pattern\\n\\nThree API groups implement both v1beta1Storage() and v1Storage() methods that register resources with different API versions:\\n\\n**1. Admission Registration (pkg/registry/admissionregistration/rest/storage_apiserver.go)**\\n- Registers validatingwebhookconfigurations, mutatingwebhookconfigurations, and admission policies in both v1 and v1beta1\\n- NewRESTStorage() calls both v1Storage() and v1beta1Storage() to register resources\\n\\n**2. Authentication (pkg/registry/authentication/rest/storage_authentication.go)**\\n- Registers tokenreviews and selfsubjectreviews in v1, with selfsubjectreviews also available in v1beta1\\n- Both versions share the same underlying storage implementation\\n\\n**3. Storage (pkg/registry/storage/rest/storage_storage.go)**\\n- Registers storageclasses, volumeattachments, csinodes, csidrivers in v1\\n- Registers volumeattributesclasses in both v1beta1 and v1\\n- The resource is stored according to v1beta1 override configured in default_storage_factory_builder.go\\n\\n## Configuration and Override System\\n\\n**1. Default Storage Factory Builder (pkg/kubeapiserver/default_storage_factory_builder.go)**\\nNewStorageFactoryConfig() creates a DefaultResourceEncodingConfig initialized from the scheme, with ResourceEncodingOverrides specifying which resources should use non-latest versions:\\n- volumeattributesclasses.storage uses v1beta1 for storage\\n- Other resources have v1alpha versions specified as overrides (coordination.leasecandidates uses v1alpha2, networking.ipaddresses and servicecidrs use v1beta1)\\n\\n**2. Resource Config Merge (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/resourceconfig/helpers.go)**\\nMergeResourceEncodingConfigs() applies GroupVersionResource overrides to DefaultResourceEncodingConfig by calling SetResourceEncoding() for each override with the external version (v1beta1, v1alpha2, etc.) and internal version.\\n\\n## Additional REST Storage Providers\\n\\nMany other API groups register only v1Storage() without v1beta1:\\n- Apps (pkg/registry/apps/rest/storage_apps.go)\\n- Authorization (pkg/registry/authorization/rest/storage_authorization.go)\\n- Autoscaling (pkg/registry/autoscaling/rest/storage_autoscaling.go)\\n- Batch, Certificates, Coordination, Discovery, Events, Networking, Policy, Scheduling (similar patterns)\\n\\nThe Resource group (pkg/registry/resource/rest/storage_resource.go) has v1alpha3Storage and v1beta1Storage but no v1Storage yet, representing an API group still in beta.\\n\\n## Flow Summary\\n\\nWhen a resource is stored in etcd:\\n1. The API server's storage factory calls NewConfig() with the GroupResource\\n2. storage_factory.go consults ResourceEncodingConfig.StorageEncodingFor()\\n3. ResourceEncodingConfig checks for SetResourceEncoding() overrides from MergeResourceEncodingConfigs()\\n4. If no override exists, it returns the highest-priority version from the scheme\\n5.
